<div class="entry-content single-content">
	<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id4696_d4ac7a-ef alignfull has-theme-palette8-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column4696_a12c78-91"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="kt-adv-heading4696_09d3c0-ee wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-2-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4696_09d3c0-ee"><mark class="kt-highlight">Create a life,</mark> <em>that feels like yours</em></h1>



<p>You don’t have to play small, or live for anyone else’s approval. <strong>I’m here to help you recognize your worth, embrace your own journey, and unlock the potential to become anything your heart desires</strong>.  With mindset tools and grounding routines, you’ll reset, grow, and step fully into the woman you’re becoming: confident, intentional, and unapologetically you.</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns4696_fc5e58-e4"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn4696_f3651f-69 kt-btn-size-standard kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-inherit  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false  wp-block-button__link wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://herlifestylepursuit.com/reset-and-refocus-map-optin/"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">get the reset &amp; refocus map</span></a></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id4696_dc026b-43 alignfull kb-v-sm-hidden has-theme-palette4-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column4696_6108c3-5c"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading4696_684e3a-ba wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4696_684e3a-ba">Intentional living and self-growth for the woman <span data-strings="[&quot;becoming her best self&quot;]" data-cursor-char="|" class="kt-typed-text">be</span></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id4696_9fb91a-d6 alignfull wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column4696_bbdd35-98"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">

<h4 class="kt-adv-heading4696_d71832-0f wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-1-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4696_d71832-0f">MEET YOUR BFF</h4>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading4696_af3d2f-6c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4696_af3d2f-6c">Hey, I’m Faith —  Your Go-to Self Growth &amp; Intentional Living BFF</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading4696_a3ba75-19 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4696_a3ba75-19"><strong>Her Lifestyle Pursuit</strong> was born out of my own journey of untangling self-doubt, perfectionism, and people-pleasing. For years, I let achievements define my worth and other people’s voices drown out my own.</p>



<p>Along the line, I’ve learned to build boundaries, trust myself, and create rhythms that feel supportive instead of draining. I know how heavy it feels to chase goals without direction or to tie your worth to constant achievements.</p>



<p>Now, I’m here to help you do the same: to recognize your worth, embrace your journey, set goals, and build based on your season, not someone else&#8217;s, and design a lifestyle that feels calm, aligned, and uniquely yours.</p>



<p>Think of me as your intentional-living BFF, here to <em>remind </em>you that you’re capable of creating a life that <em>actually </em>feels like you.</p>

<h2 class="kt-adv-heading4696_865d69-86 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4696_865d69-86">Reset &amp; Realign Kit</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading4696_da545e-41 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4696_da545e-41">A 3-part system to help you reflect on what’s working, release what’s not, and create goals that fit your life right now, not someone else’s idea of success.</p>



<p><strong>The Reset &amp; Realign Kit</strong> was made for women who are done winging it and ready to step into each month with intention. Inside, you’ll find the same tools I use to pause, reset, and realign with what matters most, so you can move forward feeling grounded and in control.</p>



<p>✨ What’s inside:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Life Reset Planner</strong> — refresh your routines with clarity</li>



<li><strong>Confidence &amp; Clarity Journal</strong> — shift your mindset and self-talk</li>



<li><strong>Balanced Goal Clarity Mini Journal</strong> — set aligned goals that fit your season</li>
</ul>
